ACTOR UtsuhoNS1Orb : FastProjectile
{
  Radius 6
  Height 12
  Speed 12
  FastSpeed 24
  damage (10)
  Projectile
  -ACTIVATEIMPACT
  -ACTIVATEPCROSS
  RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    YBL3 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    YBL3 A 0 Bright A_ScaleVelocity(1.05)
    Loop
  Death:
    YBL3 AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

    UNYU ABCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:

  MissileNormal:

ACTOR UtsuhoNS2 : Utsuho
{
  DropItem "UtsuhoMegaFlare"
  var int user_count;
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    UNYU A 0
	UNYU A 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
    UNYU BCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_FadeIn(0.075)
  Idle:
	UNYU A 1 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6124)
	UNYU A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6124,3,false)
	UNYU A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6124,70)
    UNYU BCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
	UNY2 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count", 0)
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6124)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6124,3,false)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6124,70)
	TNT1 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
    UNYU ABCDEFGHIJKLM 4 A_Chase
    Loop
  Missile:
    UNY2 PQRS 5 Fast A_FaceTarget
	UNY2 A 0 A_SetInvulnerable
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("UltraMode",1,"UltraSetup")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"MissileEasy")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	Goto MissileNormal
  UltraSetup:
	UNY2 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	Goto MissileLunatic
  MissileEasy:

ACTOR UtsuhoMegaFlare : Utsuho
{
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  DropItem "UtsuhoNS3"
  var int user_angle;
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    UNYU A 0
	UNYU A 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
    UNYU BCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_FadeIn(0.075)
  Idle:
    UNYU ABCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
	UNY2 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    UNY2 ABCDEF 5 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6125)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6125,3,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6125,60)
	UNY2 A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,62)
	UNY2 A 0 ACS_Execute(605,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNY2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/utsuho/alarm",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNY2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/utsuho/alarm",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNY2 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	UNY2 GHIHGHIHGHIJ 3 A_FaceTarget
    UNY2 KLMN 5 A_FaceTarget
	UNY2 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	UNY2 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
	UNY2 T 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", 0)
    UNYU ABCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_Chase
    Loop
  Melee:
  Missile:
    UNYU QRS 5 A_FaceTarget
    UNYU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"MissileEasy")
    UNYU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal")
    UNYU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
    UNYU A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	Goto MissileNormal
  MissileEasy:
	UNYU TU 4 A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerEasy",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU VW 4 A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerEasy",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU XY 4 A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerEasy",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU Z 0 A_SpidRefire
	Goto MissileEasy
  MissileNormal:
	UNYU TU 4 A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerNormal",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU VW 4 A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerNormal",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU XY 4 A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerNormal",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU Z 0 A_SpidRefire
	Goto MissileNormal
  MissileHard:
	UNYU TU 4 A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerHard",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU VW 4 A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerHard",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU XY 4 A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerHard",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU Z 0 A_SpidRefire
	Goto MissileHard
  MissileLunatic:
	UNYU TU 4 Fast A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,0.5,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU Z 0 A_CustomMissile("MegaFlareOrbSpawnerLunatic",frandom(16,48),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	UNYU VW 4 Fast A_FaceTarget
	UNYU Z 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)

ACTOR UtsuhoNS3Orb1 : FastProjectile
{
  Radius 6
  Height 12
  Speed 6
  FastSpeed 12
  damage (8)
  Projectile
  -ACTIVATEIMPACT
  -ACTIVATEPCROSS
  RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    YBL3 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	TNT1 A 0 Bright A_ChangeVelocity(1, 1, 0, CVF_RELATIVE)
	TNT1 A 0 Bright A_SetAngle(angle+3)
    Loop
  Death:
    YBL3 AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}
ACTOR UtsuhoNS3Orb2 : FastProjectile
{
  Radius 6
  Height 12
  Speed 6
  FastSpeed 12
  damage (8)
  Projectile
  -ACTIVATEIMPACT
  -ACTIVATEPCROSS
  RenderStyle Add

  DeathSound "touhou/hit"

  Spawn:
    YBL3 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	TNT1 A 0 Bright A_ChangeVelocity(1, -1, 0, CVF_RELATIVE)
	TNT1 A 0 Bright A_SetAngle(angle-3)
    Loop
  Death:
    YBL3 AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR UtsuhoNS4 : Utsuho

  {
  Spawn:
    UNYU A 0
	UNYU A 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
    UNYU BCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_FadeIn(0.075)
  Idle:
	UNYU A 1 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6128)
	UNYU A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6128,1,false)
	UNYU A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6128,70)
    UNYU BCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
	UNY2 T 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count", 0)
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6128)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6128,1,false)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6128,70)
	TNT1 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
    UNYU ABCDEFGHIJKLM 4 A_Chase
    Loop
  Missile:
    UNY2 PQRS 5 Fast A_FaceTarget
	UNY2 A 0 A_SetInvulnerable
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("UltraMode",1,"UltraSetup")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"MissileEasy")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	Goto MissileNormal

	UNY2 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	Goto MissileLunatic
  MissileEasy:

	UNY2 T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoNS4OrbSpawner",32,0,frandom(170,190),CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
	UNY2 T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoNS4OrbSpawner",32,0,frandom(80,100),CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
	UNY2 T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoNS4OrbSpawner",32,0,frandom(260,280),CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
	UNY2 T 6 A_SetAngle(angle+random(40,56))
	UNY2 T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoNS4OrbSpawner",32,0,frandom(-10,10),CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
	UNY2 T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoNS4OrbSpawner",32,0,frandom(170,190),CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
	UNY2 T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoNS4OrbSpawner",32,0,frandom(80,100),CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
	UNY2 T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoNS4OrbSpawner",32,0,frandom(260,280),CMF_AIMDIRECTION|CMF_TRACKOWNER)
	UNY2 T 6 A_SetAngle(angle+random(40,56))

ACTOR UtsuhoHeavenAndHellMeltdown : Utsuho
{
  Health 3000
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  //DropItem "UtsuhoSubterraneanSun"
  DropItem ""
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    UNYU A 0
	UNYU A 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
    UNYU BCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_FadeIn(0.075)
  Idle:
    UNYU ABCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
	UNY2 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    UNY2 ABCDEF 5 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6129)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6129,1,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6129,70)
	UNY2 A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,64)
	UNY2 A 0 ACS_Execute(605,0)
	UNYU T 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU T 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU T 0 A_SetAngle(0)
	UNYU T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellVisualEffectSun",32,0,90,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	UNYU T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellVisualEffectSun",32,0,270,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
	UNY2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNY2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/utsuho/alarm",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNY2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/utsuho/alarm",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNY2 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	UNY2 GHIHGHIHGHIHGHIHGHIJ 3 A_FaceTarget
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"SpellcardStartEasy")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"SpellcardStartNormal")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"SpellcardStartHard")
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"SpellcardStartLunatic")
	Goto SpellcardStartNormal
  SpellcardStartEasy:
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunEasy",0,1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunEasy",0,-1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	Goto SpellcardStartEnd
  SpellcardStartNormal:
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunNormal",0,1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunNormal",0,-1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	Goto SpellcardStartEnd
  SpellcardStartHard:
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunHard",0,1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunHard",0,-1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	Goto SpellcardStartEnd
  SpellcardStartLunatic:
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunLunatic",0,1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunLunatic",0,-1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	Goto SpellcardStartEnd
  SpellcardStartEnd:
    UNY2 KLM 6
	UNY2 K 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("UltraMode",1,"SpellcardStartUltra")
	Goto SpellcardStartEnd2
  SpellcardStartUltra:
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunLunatic",0,1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UtsuhoHeavenAndHellSpawnerSunLunatic",0,-1216,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_ABSOLUTEPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER,0)
	Goto SpellcardStartEnd2
  SpellcardStartEnd2:
	UNY2 N 6 A_FaceTarget
	UNY2 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	UNY2 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
    UNYU ABCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_Chase
    Loop
  Melee:
  Missile:
    Goto See //Utsuho herself does not shoot in this spellcard
  Death:
	UNYU N 1 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartAttack",0)
	UNYU N 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)
	UNYU N 0 ACS_Execute(603,0)
	UNYU N 0 ACS_Execute(53) //Final Spellcard requires starting in a fixed position as well
	UNYU N 0 A_GiveInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1)
    UNYU N 0 A_NoBlocking
	UNYU N 0 A_KillChildren
	UNYU N 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire")
    UNYU NNNNNNNNNN 2 A_FadeOut(0.1)
	Stop
  }
}

ACTOR UtsuhoSubterraneanSun : Utsuho //AND HERE IT IS, FINAL SPELLCARD
{
  Health 6500
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  DropItem ""
  Speed 0
  FastSpeed 0 //?!
  var int user_angle;
  var int user_phase1;
  var int user_phase2;
  DamageFactor "PlayerSpellcard", 0.05 //Basically useless
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    UNYU A 0
	UNYU A 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
    UNYU BCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_FadeIn(0.075)
  Idle:
    UNYU ABCDEFGHIJKLM 3 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
	UNY2 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"Missile")
    UNY2 ABCDEF 5 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6130)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6130,0,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimerAlternative",0,6130,150)
	UNY2 A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,65)
	UNY2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	//UNY2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/utsuho/alarm",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNY2 GHIHGHIHGHIJ 3 A_FaceTarget
    UNY2 KLMN 5 A_FaceTarget
    UNY2 PQRS 5 A_FaceTarget
	UNY2 A 0 ACS_Execute(605,0)
	UNY2 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/utsuho/alarm",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNY2 T 105 A_PlaySound("touhou/utsuho/alarm",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNYU T 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU T 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)

  Missile:

	UNYU T 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU T 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	UNY2 A 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoSubterraneanSunSun",32,0,0) //Lol at the projectile name
	UNY2 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_phase1", 99)
	Goto Missile
  GoEvenFaster:
	UNY2 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_phase2 == 99, "Missile")
	UNYU T 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
	UNYU T 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)

    UNY2 T 0 A_SetAngle(angle+13)
    UNY2 T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoSubterraneanSunSmallBullet",32,0,user_angle+random(-10,10))

	UNY2 T 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", user_angle + 10)

	UNY2 T 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", user_angle + 10)
    UNY2 T 0 A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoSubterraneanSunSmallBullet",32,0,user_angle+random(-10,10))
    UNY2 T 3 Fast A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoSubterraneanSunSmallBullet",32,0,user_angle+random(170,190))
	UNY2 T 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", user_angle + 10)
	UNY2 T 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BossTimerCheck30",1,"GoEvenFaster")
	UNY2 T 3 Fast A_JumpIfHealthLower(1000,"GoEvenFaster")
	UNY2 T 3 Fast A_JumpIfHealthLower(3000,"GoFaster")
    Goto Missile
  Death:
	UNYU N 1 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartAttack",0)
	UNYU N 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)
	UNYU N 0 ACS_Execute(603,0)
    UNYU N 0 A_GiveInventory("BulletDeathTrigger")
    UNYU N 35
	UNYU A 0 A_ScreamAndUnblock
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 BRIGHT A_SpawnItemEx("TouhouFire",frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(0,360),0,0)
	UNYU O 35
    UNYU O 0 A_Scream
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 BRIGHT A_SpawnItemEx("TouhouFireWhite",frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(0,360),0,0)
	UNYU P 35
    UNYU P 0 A_Scream
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 BRIGHT A_SpawnItemEx("TouhouFireWhite",frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(0,360),0,0)
	TNT1 A 1 ACS_Execute(116,0)
    Stop
  }
}
ACTOR UtsuhoSubterraneanSunSun
{
  Radius 12
  Speed 0
  fastspeed 0
  Height 24
  damage (20)
  Projectile
  +RIPPER
  +FORCERADIUSDMG
  +NOCLIP
  -ACTIVATEIMPACT
  -ACTIVATEPCROSS
  -MISSILE
  RenderStyle Add
  Alpha 0.75
  Scale 4.0
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    USUN A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	USUN A 0 Bright A_Explode(32,256,0)
	USUN A 0 Bright A_RadiusThrust(-24,2048,RTF_NOIMPACTDAMAGE,2048)
    Loop
  Death:
    USUN AAAAAAAAAA 4 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}
ACTOR UtsuhoSubterraneanSunBulletSpawner
{
  Radius 4
  Speed 40
  fastspeed 40
  Height 8
  damage (0)
  Projectile
  -NOBLOCKMAP
  -NOCLIP
  +THRUACTORS
  //RenderStyle Add
  //SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  //DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  DamageType "UtsuhoFire"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"AltDeath")
	Loop
  Death:
	TNT1 A 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("UtsuhoSubterraneanSunBullet",0,0,0)
    Stop
  AltDeath:
	TNT1 A 1
	Stop
  }
}

	Loop
  Death:

    Stop
  }
}
